## Analytics

 *Analytics platforms, SDK's, error tracking and real-time answers about your app*

- üåé [Aptabase](aptabase.com/for-swift) - Open Source, Privacy-First and Simple Analytics for Swift Apps.
- üåé [Answers by Fabric](get.fabric.io) - Answers gives you real-time insight into people‚Äôs experience in your app.
- üåé [Bugsnag](www.bugsnag.com/platforms/ios-crash-reporting) - Error tracking with a free tier. Error reports include data on device, release, user, and allows arbitrary data.
- üåé [Countly](count.ly) - Open source, mobile & web analytics, crash reports and push notifications platform for iOS & Android.
- üåé [devtodev](www.devtodev.com/) - Comprehensive analytics service that improves your project and saves time for product development.
- [Embrace](http://embrace.io) - Mobile observability, built on OpenTelemetry, to provide user-focused, reliable apps.
- üåé [Emerge Tools](www.emergetools.com) - Prevent app size & performance regressions on every pull request, get automated insights on how to improve.
- üåé [Instabug](instabug.com) - In-app feedback, Bug and Crash reporting, Fix Bugs Faster through user-steps, video recordings, screen annotation, network requests logging.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;400‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;169üç¥</code></b> [Matomo](https://github.com/matomo-org/matomo-sdk-ios)) - The MatomoTracker is an iOS, tvOS and macOS SDK for sending app analytics to a Matomo server.
- üåé [Mixpanel](mixpanel.com/) - Advanced analytics platform.
- üåé [MOCA Analytics](www.mocaplatform.com/features) - Paid cross-platform analytics backend.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;415‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;330üç¥</code></b> [Segment](https://github.com/segmentio/analytics-ios)) - The hassle-free way to integrate analytics into any iOS application.
- üåé [Sentry](sentry.io/) - Sentry provides self-hosted and cloud-based error monitoring that helps all software teams discover, triage, and prioritize errors in real-time.
- üåé [Shake](www.shakebugs.com/) - In-app feedback and bug reporting tool. Fix app bugs up to 50x faster with detailed device data, repro steps, video recording, black box data, network requests and custom logging.

## App Routing

  *Elegant URL routing, navigation frameworks, deep links and more*

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;852‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;71üç¥</code></b> [ApplicationCoordinator](https://github.com/AndreyPanov/ApplicationCoordinator)) - Coordinator is an object that handles navigation flow and shares flow‚Äôs handling for the next coordinator after switching on the next chain.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1182‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;77üç¥</code></b> [Appz](https://github.com/SwiftKitz/Appz)) - Easily launch and deeplink into external applications, falling back to web if not installed.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;591‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;25üç¥</code></b> [Composable Navigator](https://github.com/Bahn-X/swift-composable-navigator)) - An open source library for building deep-linkable SwiftUI applications with composition, testing and ergonomics in mind
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;424‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;23üç¥</code></b> [Crossroad](https://github.com/giginet/Crossroad)) - Crossroad is an URL router focused on handling Custom URL Schemes. Using this, you can route multiple URL schemes and fetch arguments and parameters easily.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3458‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;282üç¥</code></b> [DeepLinkKit](https://github.com/button/DeepLinkKit)) - A splendid route-matching, block-based way to handle your deep links.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5714‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;691üç¥</code></b> [JLRoutes](https://github.com/joeldev/JLRoutes)) - URL routing library for iOS with a simple block-based API.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;139‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [Linker](https://github.com/MaksimKurpa/Linker)) - Lightweight way to handle internal and external deeplinks for iOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;92‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;25üç¥</code></b> [LiteRoute](https://github.com/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute)) - Easy transition between VIPER modules, implemented on pure Swift.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;230‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;31üç¥</code></b> [Marshroute](https://github.com/avito-tech/Marshroute)) - Marshroute is an iOS Library for making your Routers simple but extremely powerful.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;919‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;63üç¥</code></b> [RouteComposer](https://github.com/ekazaev/route-composer)) - Library that helps to handle view controllers composition, routing and deeplinking tasks.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;447‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26üç¥</code></b> [Router](https://github.com/freshOS/Router)) - Simple Navigation for iOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1899‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;115üç¥</code></b> [RxFlow](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxFlow)) - Navigation framework for iOS applications based on a Reactive Flow Coordinator pattern.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;306‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [SwiftCurrent](https://github.com/wwt/SwiftCurrent)) - A library for managing complex workflows.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;280‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;28üç¥</code></b> [SwiftRouter](https://github.com/skyline75489/SwiftRouter)) - A URL Router for iOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3338‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;296üç¥</code></b> [URLNavigator](https://github.com/devxoul/URLNavigator)) - Elegant URL Routing for Swift
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;586‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;27üç¥</code></b> [WAAppRouting](https://github.com/Wasappli/WAAppRouting)) - iOS routing done right. Handles both URL recognition and controller displaying with parsed parameters. All in one line, controller stack preserved automatically!
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;662‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;115üç¥</code></b> [ZIKRouter](https://github.com/Zuikyo/ZIKRouter)) - An interface-oriented router for discovering modules and injecting dependencies with protocol in OC & Swift, iOS & macOS. Handles route in a type safe way.

## App Store

*Apple Guidelines and version notification libraries*

- üåé [Apple Review Guidelines](developer.apple.com/app-store/review/#common-app-rejections) - Highlighted some of the most common issues that cause apps to get rejected.
- üåé [Free App Store Optimization Tool](www.mobileaction.co) - Lets you track your App Store visibility in terms of keywords and competitors.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4297‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;418üç¥</code></b> [Siren](https://github.com/ArtSabintsev/Siren)) - Notify users when a new version of your app is available and prompt them to upgrade.

## Apple TV

*tvOS view controllers, wrappers, template managers and video players.*

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;77‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26üç¥</code></b> [FocusTvButton](https://github.com/dcordero/FocusTvButton)) - Light wrapper of UIButton that allows extra customization for tvOS
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;487‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;51üç¥</code></b> [ParallaxView](https://github.com/PGSSoft/ParallaxView)) - iOS controls and extensions that add parallax effect to your application.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;82‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;25üç¥</code></b> [Swift-GA-Tracker-for-Apple-tvOS](https://github.com/adswerve/Swift-GA-Tracker-for-Apple-tvOS)) - Google Analytics tracker for Apple tvOS provides an easy integration of Google Analytics‚Äô measurement protocol for Apple TV.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;32‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [TvOSCustomizableTableViewCell](https://github.com/zattoo/TvOSCustomizableTableViewCell)) - Light wrapper of UITableViewCell that allows extra customization for tvOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;61‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [TvOSMoreButton](https://github.com/cgoldsby/TvOSMoreButton)) - A basic tvOS button which truncates long text with '... More'.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;102‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [TvOSPinKeyboard](https://github.com/zattoo/TvOSPinKeyboard)) - PIN keyboard for tvOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;182‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [TvOSScribble](https://github.com/dcordero/TvOSScribble)) - Handwriting numbers recognizer for Siri Remote.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;47‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [TvOSSlider](https://github.com/zattoo/TvOSSlider)) - TvOSSlider is an implementation of UISlider for tvOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;49‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [TvOSTextViewer](https://github.com/dcordero/TvOSTextViewer)) - Light and scrollable view controller for tvOS to present blocks of text
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2935‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;621üç¥</code></b> [XCDYouTubeKit](https://github.com/0xced/XCDYouTubeKit)) - YouTube video player for iOS, tvOS and macOS.

## Architecture Patterns

*Clean architecture, Viper, MVVM, Reactive... choose your weapon.*

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6379‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;782üç¥</code></b> [Clean Architecture for SwiftUI + Combine](https://github.com/nalexn/clean-architecture-swiftui)) - A demo project showcasing the production setup of the SwiftUI app with Clean Architecture.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4046‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;504üç¥</code></b> [CleanArchitectureRxSwift](https://github.com/sergdort/CleanArchitectureRxSwift)) - Example of Clean Architecture of iOS app using RxSwift.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1530‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;187üç¥</code></b> [ios-architecture](https://github.com/tailec/ios-architecture)) - A collection of iOS architectures - MVC, MVVM, MVVM+RxSwift, VIPER, RIBs and many others.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;734‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;181üç¥</code></b> [iOS-Viper-Architecture](https://github.com/MindorksOpenSource/iOS-Viper-Architecture)) - This repository contains a detailed sample app that implements VIPER architecture in iOS using libraries and frameworks like Alamofire, AlamofireImage, PKHUD, CoreData etc.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;371‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [Reactant](https://github.com/Brightify/Reactant)) - Reactant is a reactive architecture for iOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;124‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [Spin](https://github.com/Spinners/Spin.Swift)) - A universal implementation of a Feedback Loop system for RxSwift, ReactiveSwift and Combine
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;124‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;15üç¥</code></b> [SwiftyVIPER](https://github.com/codytwinton/SwiftyVIPER)) - Makes implementing VIPER architecture much easier and cleaner.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;722‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;33üç¥</code></b> [Tempura](https://github.com/BendingSpoons/tempura-swift)) - A holistic approach to iOS development, inspired by Redux and MVVM.
- <b><code>&nbsp;14005‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1598üç¥</code></b> [The Composable Architecture](https://github.com/pointfreeco/swift-composable-architecture)) - The Composable Architecture is a library for building applications in a consistent and understandable way, with composition, testing, and ergonomics in mind.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;78‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [VIPER Module Generator](https://github.com/Kaakati/VIPER-Module-Generator)) - A Clean VIPER Modules Generator with comments and predfined functions.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;513‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;69üç¥</code></b> [Viperit](https://github.com/ferranabello/Viperit)) - Viper Framework for iOS. Develop an app following VIPER architecture in an easy way. Written and tested in Swift.

**[back to top](#contributing-and-collaborating)**

## ARKit

*Library and tools to help you build unparalleled augmented reality experiences*

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;130‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10üç¥</code></b> [ARHeadsetKit](https://github.com/philipturner/ARHeadsetKit)) - High-level framework for using $5 Google Cardboard to replicate
 Microsoft Hololens.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5521‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;733üç¥</code></b> [ARKit-CoreLocation](https://github.com/ProjectDent/ARKit-CoreLocation)) - Combines the high accuracy of AR with the scale of GPS data.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;545‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;59üç¥</code></b> [ARKit Emperor](https://github.com/kboy-silvergym/ARKit-Emperor)) - The Emperor give you the most practical ARKit samples ever.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;379‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;83üç¥</code></b> [ARKit Virtual Objects](https://github.com/ignacio-chiazzo/ARKit)) - Placing Virtual Objects in Augmented Reality.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1657‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;225üç¥</code></b> [ARVideoKit](https://github.com/AFathi/ARVideoKit)) - Record and capture ARKit videos, photos, Live Photos, and GIFs.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;99‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [Placenote](https://github.com/Placenote/PlacenoteSDK-iOS)) - A library that makes ARKit sessions persistent to a location using advanced computer vision.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;629‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34üç¥</code></b> [SmileToUnlock](https://github.com/rsrbk/SmileToUnlock)) - This library uses ARKit Face Tracking in order to catch a user's smile.

## Authentication

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;642‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;86üç¥</code></b> [Heimdallr.swift](https://github.com/trivago/Heimdallr.swift)) - Easy to use OAuth 2 library for iOS, written in Swift.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;94‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20üç¥</code></b> [InstagramSimpleOAuth](https://github.com/rbaumbach/InstagramSimpleOAuth)) - A quick and simple way to authenticate an Instagram user in your iPhone or iPad app.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;37‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [LinkedInSignIn](https://github.com/serhii-londar/LinkedInSignIn)) - Simple view controller to login and retrieve access token from LinkedIn.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1177‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;284üç¥</code></b> [OAuth2](https://github.com/p2/OAuth2)) - OAuth2 framework for macOS and iOS, written in Swift.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3320‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;599üç¥</code></b> [OAuthSwift](https://github.com/OAuthSwift/OAuthSwift)) - Swift based OAuth library for iOS
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;271‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;136üç¥</code></b> [ReCaptcha](https://github.com/fjcaetano/ReCaptcha)) - (In)visible ReCaptcha for iOS.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;485‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;30üç¥</code></b> [SwiftyOAuth](https://github.com/delba/SwiftyOAuth)) - A simple OAuth library for iOS with a built-in set of providers.

## Blockchain

*Tool for smart contract interactions. Bitcoin protocol implementations and Frameworks for interacting with cryptocurrencies.*

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;866‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;291üç¥</code></b> [BitcoinKit](https://github.com/yenom/BitcoinKit)) - Bitcoin protocol toolkit for Swift, BitcoinKit implements Bitcoin protocol in Swift. It is an implementation of the Bitcoin SPV protocol written in swift.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [CoinpaprikaAPI](https://github.com/coinpaprika/coinpaprika-api-swift-client)) - Coinpaprika API client with free & frequently updated market data from the world of crypto: coin prices, volumes, market caps, ATHs, return rates and more.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;487‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;100üç¥</code></b> [EthereumKit](https://github.com/yuzushioh/EthereumKit)) - EthereumKit is a free, open-source Swift framework for easily interacting with the Ethereum.

## Cache

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1273‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;167üç¥</code></b> [Awesome Cache](https://github.com/aschuch/AwesomeCache)) - Delightful on-disk cache (written in Swift).

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;642‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;33üç¥</code></b> [Carlos](https://github.com/spring-media/Carlos)) - A simple but flexible cache.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3124‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;174üç¥</code></b> [Disk](https://github.com/saoudrizwan/Disk)) - Delightful framework for iOS to easily persist structs, images, and data.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5186‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;587üç¥</code></b> [HanekeSwift](https://github.com/Haneke/HanekeSwift)) - A lightweight generic cache for iOS written in Swift with extra love for images.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;37‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [Johnny](https://github.com/zolomatok/Johnny)) - Melodic Caching for Swift.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;647‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;50üç¥</code></b> [RocketData](https://github.com/plivesey/RocketData)) - A caching and consistency solution for immutable models.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1247‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;77üç¥</code></b> [SPTPersistentCache](https://github.com/spotify/SPTPersistentCache)) - Everyone tries to implement a cache at some point in their iOS app‚Äôs lifecycle, and this is ours. By Spotify.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;270‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20üç¥</code></b> [Track](https://github.com/maquannene/Track)) - Track is a thread safe cache write by Swift. Composed of DiskCache and MemoryCache which support LRU.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;75‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [UITableView Cache](https://github.com/Kilograpp/UITableView-Cache)) - UITableView cell cache that cures scroll-lags on a cell instantiating.

## Localization

*Tools to manage strings files, translate and enable localization in your apps.*

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;542‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57üç¥</code></b> [Hodor](https://github.com/Aufree/Hodor)) - Simple solution to localize your iOS App.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1404‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;120üç¥</code></b> [BartyCrouch](https://github.com/Flinesoft/BartyCrouch)) - Incrementally update/translate your Strings files from Code and Storyboards/XIBs.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1221‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;79üç¥</code></b> [LocalizationKit](https://github.com/willpowell8/LocalizationKit_iOS)) - Localization management in realtime from a web portal. Easily manage your texts and translations without redeploy and resubmission.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;3115‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;328üç¥</code></b> [Localize-Swift](https://github.com/marmelroy/Localize-Swift)) - Swift 2.0 friendly localization and i18n with in-app language switching.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;301‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;35üç¥</code></b> [AsyncMessagesViewController](https://github.com/nguyenhuy/AsyncMessagesViewController)) - A smooth, responsive and flexible messages UI library for iOS.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;4505‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;595üç¥</code></b> [Chatto](https://github.com/badoo/Chatto)) - A lightweight framework to build chat applications, made in Swift.

## Notifications

### Push Notifications

## Reflection
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;596‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;42üç¥</code></b> [Reflection](https://github.com/Zewo/Reflection)) - Reflection provides an API for advanced reflection at runtime including dynamic construction of types.

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;447‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;39üç¥</code></b> [JSONNeverDie](https://github.com/johnlui/JSONNeverDie)) - Auto reflection tool from JSON to Model, user friendly JSON encoder / decoder, aims to never die.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;135‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [SwiftKVC](https://github.com/bradhilton/SwiftKVC)) - Key-Value Coding (KVC) for native Swift classes and structs.

## Xcode

### Extensions

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;186‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;15üç¥</code></b> [CleanClosureXcode](https://github.com/BalestraPatrick/CleanClosureXcode)) - An Xcode Source Editor extension to clean the closure syntax.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [xTextHandler](https://github.com/cyanzhong/xTextHandler)) - Xcode Source Editor Extension Toolset (Plugins for Xcode 8).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;717‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;31üç¥</code></b> [SwiftInitializerGenerator](https://github.com/Bouke/SwiftInitializerGenerator)) - Xcode 8 Source Code Extension to Generate Swift Initializers.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;188‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16üç¥</code></b> [XcodeEquatableGenerator](https://github.com/sergdort/XcodeEquatableGenerator)) - Xcode 8 Source Code Extension will generate conformance to Swift Equatable protocol based on type and fields selection.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;843‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40üç¥</code></b> [Import](https://github.com/markohlebar/Import)) - Xcode extension for adding imports from anywhere in the code.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;158‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [Mark](https://github.com/velyan/Mark)) - Xcode extension for generating MARK comments.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;73‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [XShared](https://github.com/Otbivnoe/XShared)) - Xcode extension which allows you copying the code with special formatting quotes for social (Slack, Telegram).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;81‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [XGist](https://github.com/Bunn/Xgist)) - Xcode extension which allows you to send your text selection or entire file to GitHub's Gist and automatically copy the Gist URL into your Clipboard.
* üåé [Swiftify](swiftify.com/) - Objective-C to Swift online code converter and Xcode extension.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;35‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [DocumenterXcode](https://github.com/serhii-londar/DocumenterXcode)) - Attempt to give a new life for VVDocumenter-Xcode as source editor extension.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;107‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [Snowonder](https://github.com/Karetski/Snowonder)) - Magical import declarations formatter for Xcode.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2299‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;177üç¥</code></b> [XVim2](https://github.com/XVimProject/XVim2)) - Vim key-bindings for Xcode 9.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;160‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [Comment Spell Checker](https://github.com/velyan/Comment-Spell-Checker)) - Xcode extension for spell checking and auto correcting code comments.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;202‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [nef](https://github.com/bow-swift/nef-plugin)) - This Xcode extension enables you to make a code selection and export it to a snippets. Available on Mac AppStore.

### Other Xcode

- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;127‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [awesome-xcode-scripts](https://github.com/aashishtamsya/awesome-xcode-scripts)) - A curated list of useful xcode scripts.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;6062‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;271üç¥</code></b> [Synx](https://github.com/venmo/synx)) - A command-line tool that reorganizes your Xcode project folder to match your Xcode groups.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [dsnip](https://github.com/Tintenklecks/IBDelegateCodesippets)) - Tool to generate (native) Xcode code snippets from all protocols/delegate methods of UIKit (UITableView, ...)
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1742‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;164üç¥</code></b> [SBShortcutMenuSimulator](https://github.com/DeskConnect/SBShortcutMenuSimulator)) - 3D Touch shortcuts in the Simulator.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [awesome-gitignore-templates](https://github.com/aashishtamsya/awesome-gitignore-templates)) - A collection of swift, objective-c, android and many more langugages .gitignore templates.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;89‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [swift-project-template](https://github.com/artemnovichkov/swift-project-template)) - Template for iOS Swift project generation.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;545‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;109üç¥</code></b> [Swift-VIPER-Module](https://github.com/Juanpe/Swift-VIPER-Module)) - Xcode template for create modules with VIPER Architecture written in Swift 3.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;80‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;24üç¥</code></b> [ViperC](https://github.com/abdullahselek/ViperC)) - Xcode template for VIPER Architecture for both Objective-C and Swift.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [XcodeCodeSnippets](https://github.com/ismetanin/XcodeCodeSnippets)) - A set of code snippets for iOS development, includes code and comments snippets.
- üåé [Xcode Keymap for Visual Studio Code](marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=stevemoser.xcode-keybindings) - This extension ports popular Xcode keyboard shortcuts to Visual Studio Code.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [Xcode Template Manager](https://github.com/Camji55/xtm)) - Xcode Template Manager is a Swift command line tool that helps you manage your Xcode project templates.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [VIPER Module Template](https://github.com/EvsenevDev/VIPERModuleTemplate)) - Xcode Template of VIPER Module which generates all layers of VIPER.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;312‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40üç¥</code></b> [Xcode Developer Disk Images](https://github.com/haikieu/xcode-developer-disk-image-all-platforms)) - Xcode Developer Disk Images is needed when you want to put your build to the device, however sometimes your Xcode is not updated with the latest Disk Images, you could find them here for convenience.
- <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2404‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;104üç¥</code></b> [Swift Macros üöÄ](https://github.com/krzysztofzablocki/Swift-Macros)) - A curated list of community-created Macros and associated learning resources.
